TI MOLECULAR AND CRYSTAL-STRUCTURES OF 5-NITROFURAN-2-ALDOXIME AND
   THIOPHENE ANALOGS AS SHG MATERIALS
SO CHEMISTRY LETTERS
LA English
DT Article
AB 5-Nitrofuran-2-aldoxime (1b) exhibits crystallographic polymorphism.  The isolated two crystals show SHG efficiency of 12 and 3 times that of urea.  5-Nitrothiophene-2-aldoxime (2b) shows weak SHG response because of the hypervalent interactions of O-S-O atoms.  Two crystals of 1b and 2b belong to P2(1)2(1)2(1) space group.
C1 KWANSEI GAKUIN UNIV,COLL SCI,DEPT CHEM,NISHINOMIYA,HYOGO 662,JAPAN.

TI THE X-RAY-EMISSION OF SS-433
SO ASTRONOMY & ASTROPHYSICS
LA English
DT Article
DE X-RAYS, BINARIES; BLACK HOLES; NEUTRON STARS; SUPERNOVA REMNANTS;
   X-RAYS, SPECTROSCOPY
ID SS 433; SS433; MODEL; EVOLUTION; BINARIES; GINGA; JETS; LINE; MOTIONS;
   ECLIPSE
AB Recent X-ray observations of SS 433 with the Ginga satellite, centered at the phases of optical primary minimum revealed new information about the systems properties. The main observational result is that the spectrum of the source is extremely hard, best fitted with a thermal bremsstrahlung law with kT less-than-or-similar-to 30 keV, which softens during eclipse to kT almost-equal-to 12 keV. The 6.7 keV iron line region appears to be very complex and varies with the processional phase.
   It is argued that the X-ray flux from the jets is strongly modulated by large structures on the disc. If these can be modelled properly they will provide important clues to the disc's physical properties which might lead to a better understanding of the precession mechanism.

TI TEMPERATURE-DEPENDENCE OF POLARITON LUMINESCENCE IN CUCL
SO JOURNAL OF LUMINESCENCE
LA English
DT Article; Proceedings Paper
CT 1990 INTERNATIONAL CONF ON LUMINESCENCE ( ICL 90 )
CY JUL 16-20, 1990
CL LISBON, PORTUGAL
SP CALOUSTE GULBENKIAN FDN
ID CDS
AB We have studied the time-integrated spectra and temporal behavior of Z3-exciton-polariton luminescence in the temperature range from 4 to 88 K under excitation at the Z1,2-exciton absorption region.  The temperature-dependent spatial motion of polaritons at each temperature modifies the temporal behavior of polariton luminescence significantly.  The observed results show that the polariton motion changes from the free propagative one at low temperature to the diffusive one at high temperature.  The lifetime of polaritons becomes longer with increasing temperature.

TI MORPHOLOGY OF ORIENTED CALCIUM ALGINATE GELS OBTAINED BY THE
   FLOW-GELATION METHOD
SO POLYMER
LA English
DT Article
DE CALCIUM ALGINATE; FLOW; GELATION; BIREFRINGENCE; MORPHOLOGY
ID CONFORMATIONAL ENERGY CALCULATIONS; X-RAY-DIFFRACTION; STRUCTURAL
   COMPONENTS; CRYSTALLINE-STRUCTURE; ACID
AB Cylinder-shaped oriented gels of calcium alginate were prepared by extruding a 2.6 wt% aqueous solution of sodium alginate (guluronate rich) into CaCl2 solution through a glass tube. Effects of flow rates on chain orientation in solution and in the gel were examined by polarized optical microscopy. During flow, chains underwent planar orientation along the tube wall, which was reflected in the gel state. Increasing the flow rate increased the coil stretch transition in solution but led to disorientation of chains in the gel due to increasing die swell and longitudinal shrinkage. This effect resulted in the occurrence of the highest anisotropy of the gel at low flow rate. Chain orientation in the gel was characterized by tilting towards the tangential direction with the appearance of a small negative birefringence, which was transformed to a large positive birefringence on drying due to chain realignment in the longitudinal direction. The morphology of the gel was deduced to be sheet-like structures stacked cylindrically with strong intrasheet binding. Scanning electron microscopy and wide-angle X-ray diffraction were both used in the investigation.
RP YOKOYAMA, F (reprint author), OKAYAMA UNIV,FAC ENGN,DEPT APPL CHEM,OKAYAMA 700,JAPAN.

TI ESR SENSITIVITY COMPARISON OF SUGAR FROM VARIOUS SOURCES AND CAVITY MODE
   EFFECT
SO RADIATION PROTECTION DOSIMETRY
LA English
DT Article; Proceedings Paper
CT 9TH INTERNATIONAL CONF ON SOLID STATE DOSIMETRY
CY NOV 06-10, 1989
CL VIENNA, AUSTRIA
SP AUSTRIAN RES CTR
AB Sugar is a suitable material for ESR dosimetry in emergency situations and for high dose dosemeters.  The radiation properties of sugar produced in twenty-six countries have been studied, but no differences among them was observed.  A minimum detectable dose using the sugar ESR dosemeter was about 5 mGy, which was determined by comparison of the ESR absorption intensity between non-irradiated and irradiated sugars.  A preliminary international dose intercomparison between Thailand and Japan using the sugar ESR dosemeter was tried.  An ESR instrument with two different microwave cavities of TE011 and TM110 modes used in this work could detect free radicals in the irradiated sugar.
RP NAKAJIMA, T (reprint author), NATL INST RADIOL SCI,CHIBA 260,JAPAN.
